Result: 最佳模型在15个标签类别上实现了88.67%的词级准确率和81.67%的宏平均F1分数。数据集、标注指南和训练模型检查点已公开发布。

Conclusion: L3Cube-MahaPOS是马拉地语自然语言处理领域的重要资源，为未来研究提供了高质量基准，有助于推动马拉地语在机器翻译、信息抽取和句法分析等任务中的发展。

Abstract: Part-of-Speech (POS) tagging is a foundational NLP task underpinning machine translation, information extraction, and syntactic parsing. Despite Marathi being spoken by over 83 million people and ranking among the top twenty most spoken languages worldwide, it remains severely under-resourced in annotated corpora and standardised evaluation benchmarks. Marathi presents unique challenges for computational modelling owing to its rich morphology, relatively free word order, lack of capitalisation conventions, and pervasive code-mixing with Hindi and English. We introduce L3Cube-MahaPOS, a gold-standard POS tagging dataset for Marathi comprising 32,354 manually annotated sentences drawn from news text. Annotation was performed entirely manually by a team of Marathi-proficient annotators following a 16-tag Universal Dependencies-aligned scheme. A structured preprocessing pipeline covering Unicode normalisation, Devanagari-aware tokenisation, and noise filtering ensures label consistency across all splits. We benchmark the dataset across six model families spanning HMM, CRF, BiLSTM, BiLSTM+CharCNN, MuRIL, and the Marathi-specific transformer MahaBERT-v2. The best system achieves 88.67\% token-level accuracy and a macro-F1 of 81.67% over 15 evaluated tag classes. We release the dataset, annotation guidelines, and trained model checkpoints to foster further research in Marathi NLP.

### [184] [Less is More: Quality-Aware Training Data Selection for Scientific Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24828)
*Maria Nefeli Paraskevopoulou,Tatiana Passali,Grigorios Tsoumakas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文构建并发布了一个包含188万篇PMC文章的大型生物医学和生命科学长文档摘要数据集，解决了现有数据集规模小、结构不适应现代长上下文模型的问题。同时，通过基于源文本和模型的评估指标分析作者撰写的摘要质量，发现其与原文的对齐程度不一，并提出利用质量信号进行高质量子集选择，训练效果优于随机采样，甚至可超越更大规模的随机子集，在事实性指标上表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学长文档摘要数据集普遍将作者撰写的摘要作为黄金参考摘要，但其质量和与原文的对齐程度存在差异；同时，公开可用的数据集在规模和结构上仍不足以支持现代长上下文模型的训练需求。

Method: 构建并发布大规模生物医学与生命科学长文档摘要数据集（188万篇PMC文章），采用源基和模型驱动的度量方法评估作者摘要的质量，基于质量信号筛选高质量训练数据子集，并对比不同采样策略的模型性能。

Result: 作者撰写的摘要在与全文的对齐程度上存在显著差异；基于质量信号选择的高质量子集在相同训练规模下优于随机采样，且在事实性相关指标上可达到或超过更大的随机子集表现。

Conclusion: 参考摘要的质量是科学摘要任务中的重要因素，采用质量感知的数据选择策略能够有效提升训练效率与模型性能。

Abstract: Scientific long-document summarization datasets commonly treat author-written abstracts as gold reference summaries, although their quality and alignment with the source article vary. At the same time, publicly available scientific summarization datasets remain limited in scale and structure for modern long-context models. In this work, we address both challenges by a) constructing and releasing one of the largest biomedical and life science datasets for long-document summarization, containing 1.88 million PMC articles, and b) analyzing the reference quality of author-written abstracts with source-grounded and model-based metrics. We show that author-written abstracts vary in their alignment with the full article and that these quality signals can guide training-data selection. Training on selected high-quality subsets outperforms random sampling at matched training sizes and can match or exceed larger random subsets on factuality-oriented metrics. Our findings suggest that reference quality is an important factor in scientific summarization and that quality-aware data selection can improve training efficiency.

### [185] [Systematic Exploration of 4-Expert Heterogeneous Mixture-of-Experts via Automated Pipeline Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23739)
*Yashkumar R Lukhi,Harsh Rameshbhai Moradiya,Radu Timofte,Dmitry Ignatov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种自动化的大规模搜索流水线，用于在LEMUR神经网络数据生态系统中探索异构4-专家混合专家（MoE4）架构。该流水线基于手写异构MoE参考模型，用确定性代码生成器替代人工设计，系统性地组合来自LEMUR数据库的基线架构家族，形成由卷积门控网络控制的MoE4集成模型，并采用温度缩放、mixup增强和余弦退火学习率调度。在NVIDIA RTX 4090上运行28天，共生成4,463个候选模型，成功评估1,021个。关键发现：由于itertools.combinations的字母顺序枚举，整个探索空间（理论23,751种组合的4.8%）锚定于单一架构AirNet，存在显著覆盖偏差。分析指出根源在于生成器，提出分层随机采样修正方案。在以AirNet为锚点的范围内，ShuffleNet与MobileNetV3持续产生最高精度集成模型（平均准确率高达0.632），而FractalNet和MNASNet被识别为低产出家族，建议未来排除。相关流水线、分析结果及修正后的生成器已作为开源项目NNGPT发布于GitHub。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统手动设计异构混合专家（MoE）架构效率低且易受偏见影响。为实现大规模、系统性探索，需构建自动化搜索流水线，避免人为引入的结构偏差，提升模型发现效率与可重复性。

Method: 基于手写异构MoE参考模型，使用确定性代码生成器，从LEMUR数据库中系统组合不同基线架构家族，形成MoE4集成模型；每个模型由卷积门控网络控制，结合温度缩放、mixup数据增强和余弦退火学习率调度进行训练；通过28天大规模实验，在NVIDIA RTX 4090上生成并评估数千个候选模型。

Result: 发现因itertools.combinations的字母顺序枚举导致搜索空间严重锚定于AirNet，仅覆盖理论组合的4.8%，存在显著偏差；在该受限空间内，ShuffleNet与MobileNetV3组合表现最优（平均准确率达0.632），而FractalNet与MNASNet为低产出家族。提出分层随机采样方法修正生成器偏差。

Conclusion: 自动化搜索流水线虽有效生成大量候选模型，但其底层生成逻辑可能引入隐蔽的覆盖偏差。本研究揭示了这一问题的根源并提出可复现的修正策略，强调在大规模架构搜索中需对采样机制进行严格验证。相关成果已开源，可供后续研究复用与改进。

Abstract: We present an automated large-scale search pipeline for heterogeneous 4-Expert Mixture-of-Experts (MoE4) architectures within the LEMUR neural network dataset ecosystem. Building on a hand-crafted heterogeneous MoE reference model, we replace manual design with a deterministic code-assembly generator that systematically combines base architecture families drawn from the LEMUR database into MoE4 ensembles, each governed by a convolutional gating network with temperature scaling, mixup augmentation, and cosine-annealed learning rate scheduling. Over a 28-day campaign on an NVIDIA RTX 4090, the pipeline generated 4,463 candidate models across 197 batches, of which 1,021 were evaluated successfully. A critical finding emerged from the campaign: due to alphabetical enumeration via itertools.combinations, the entire explored search space (4.8% of the theoretical 23,751 possible 4-family combinations) is anchored to a single family, AirNet. We characterise this coverage bias precisely, identify the root cause in the generator, and propose a stratified random sampling fix. Within the AirNet anchored scope, ShuffleNet and MobileNetV3 consistently co-produce the highest-accuracy ensembles (mean accuracy up to 0.632), while FractalNet and MNASNet are identified as low-yield families warranting exclusion in future campaigns. The pipeline, analysis artefacts, and corrected generator are released as part of the open-source NNGPT project at https://github.com/ABrain-One/nn-gpt

</details>


### [186] [Weight-Space Geometry of Offline Reasoning Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23740)
*Aleksandr Nikolich,Igor Kiselev,Vladimir Platonov,Karina Romanova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究比较了六种离线强化学习损失函数（SFT, RFT, DFT, RIFT, Offline GRPO, DPO）在相同数学推理数据上的权重更新差异，发现尽管它们在下游准确率上表现相似，但机制上存在显著区别。SFT、RFT和RIFT的权重变化几乎共线，而DFT方向偏离较大；Offline GRPO引入了大量正交于SFT方向的更新，尤其在深层网络中；DPO则处于近乎正交的子空间，表现出模式连接性障碍，并在准确率上显著领先，但其优势可能源于更小的学习率与损失函数的联合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离线强化学习方法常仅以下游任务准确率为标准进行比较，但缺乏对这些方法是否在机制上具有本质区别的深入分析。本文旨在探究不同损失函数是否导致相似或不同的权重更新路径，从而揭示其内在机制差异。

Method: 在相同基模型Qwen3-4B上使用注意力仅限的LoRA训练六种方法，基于相同的数学推理轨迹数据，通过余弦相似度、主角子空间分析、线性模式连接性和核相关性分析（CKA）评估权重更新的几何结构差异。

Result: (i) SFT、RFT和RIFT的权重变化高度共线（余弦相似度≥0.97，主角中位数约7度），准确率相近（GSM8K 87–88%）；(ii) DFT虽用相同数据，但方向偏离最远；(iii) Offline GRPO引入显著正交分量（全局约67%，深层达86%），但仍位于SFT损失盆地内；(iv) DPO位于近正交子空间，模式连接性差，晚期层CKA降至0.46，准确率最高（GSM8K 93.5%，AIME26 30.0%），但其优势可能来自更低学习率与损失函数的共同作用。

Conclusion: 不同离线强化学习损失函数在权重更新方向上存在显著机制差异，即使在相同数据和任务下，也未收敛至同一更新路径。这表明下游性能相近并不意味着机制等价，应结合几何结构分析理解模型优化行为。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement-learning losses (RFT, RIFT, DFT, Offline GRPO, DPO) are widely used to distill reasoning from large teachers into smaller students, and are typically compared on downstream accuracy alone. We ask whether they are mechanistically distinct or converge to a similar weight update. Training six methods (SFT, RFT, DFT, RIFT, Offline GRPO, DPO) on identical math rollouts from a single base model (Qwen3-4B) with attention-only LoRA, we analyze the resulting deltas via cosine similarity, principal-angle subspace analysis, linear mode connectivity, and CKA. We observe: (i) SFT, RFT, and RIFT have nearly colinear weight deltas (cosine >= 0.97, top-1 principal angle ~7 deg median over 144 modules) and comparable GSM8K accuracy (87-88%, n=1319; pairwise McNemar p >= 0.15); (ii) DFT diverges further in direction than any reward-weighted method despite using the same data; (iii) Offline GRPO adds a substantial component orthogonal to the SFT direction (~67% globally, up to ~86% in late layers) while staying in the SFT loss basin; (iv) DPO sits in a near-orthogonal subspace, shows a mode-connectivity barrier, and collapses late-layer CKA to ~0.46. DPO also reaches the highest accuracy in our protocol on both GSM8K (93.5%, McNemar p < 10^-9 vs. each other method) and AIME26 (30.0% vs. 3.3-10.0%); its training uses a 10x smaller learning rate than the others (the standard convention), so the update-norm and accuracy gaps reflect loss-function and optimizer choices jointly, and a learning-rate-matched DPO comparison is left for future work.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Causal reasoning, which encompasses the discovery of causal structures and the inference of causal effects, is fundamental to data-driven decision making. In practice, data for reliable causal analysis are often distributed across institutions and cannot be centralized due to privacy regulations or communication constraints. Federated learning (FL) addresses this by enabling collaborative analysis without raw data sharing, giving rise to the rapidly growing field of federated causal discovery (FCD) and inference (FCI). However, the interdisciplinary nature of this field and the absence of a comprehensive survey present barriers to entry for researchers. This paper bridges that gap by providing a systematic review through multi-dimensional taxonomies. Grounded in the three core design decisions underlying any FCD solution, namely how structures are learned, how data are partitioned, and what structural knowledge each party obtains, we organize FCD along three axes: methodological paradigm, federation topology, and structural scope. We further examine key practical dimensions, including temporal dynamics, data heterogeneity, missing data, and non-identical variable sets. For FCI, we categorize methods by target estimand (average versus individualized/conditional treatment effects) and by estimation strategy, from classical weighting methods to modern deep generative architectures. Unlike prior works that treat FCD and FCI separately, we formalize their connection as complementary stages of a unified federated causal reasoning pipeline, where FCD supplies the structural knowledge required for valid effect estimation in FCI. Finally, we highlight their shared concerns regarding privacy, communication efficiency, theoretical guarantees, and application domains, and conclude by identifying open challenges for future research.

### [188] [Low-power analogue neural networks with trainable nonlinear connections for continuous control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23742)
*Ian T. Vidamour,Fernando Aguirre,Thomas J. Hayward,Matthew O. A. Ellis,Charles Swindells,Alexander McDonnell,Martin Trefzer,Finley Robins,Luca Manneschi,Susan Stepney,Tony Kenyon,Oliver J. Sutton,Jack C. Gartside,Ivan Y. Tyukin,Adnan Mehonic,Eleni Vasilaki*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种新型物理神经网络架构，将可训练的非线性函数置于连接上，而非传统方式将其作为标量权重。利用模拟带通滤波器在可编程模拟阵列上实现，该方法在处理平滑连续目标（如机器人运动学、连续控制和光伏最大功率点追踪）时显著减少节点和连接数量，但对分类任务无优势。网络可在约35,000个连接上实现硬件迁移，并具备量化保真度；专用CMOS实现预计功耗仅约30微瓦。忆阻器仿真验证了该优势源于连接上的可训练非线性，而非特定器件特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理神经网络受限于将非线性器件响应当作标量权重，限制了计算灵活性。为提升效率与表达能力，受Kolmogorov-Arnold网络启发，提出将可训练非线性函数置于连接上，以增强对平滑连续任务的建模能力。

Method: 在可编程模拟阵列上使用模拟带通滤波器实现连接上的可训练非线性函数，构建新型物理神经网络；通过硬件实验与仿真验证其性能，包括网络迁移能力、能效表现及忆阻器实现的兼容性。

Result: 对于平滑连续任务，该网络显著降低所需节点和连接数；在硬件上实现跨约35,000连接的高保真迁移；专用CMOS设计预计功耗为30微瓦；忆阻器仿真再现相同行为，证明优势源自结构设计而非具体器件。

Conclusion: 将可训练非线性函数置于连接上，是提升物理神经网络在连续任务中参数效率的关键，且该优势具有器件无关性，为低功耗机器学习提供了新路径。

Abstract: Physical neural networks promise low-power machine learning by computing directly with analogue device physics, but most architectures force nonlinear device responses to act as scalar weights. Inspired by Kolmogorov-Arnold networks, we place trainable nonlinear functions on the connections, making each physical connection a learnable computational element. Realising these functions as analogue band-pass filters on field-programmable analogue arrays, we find that the benefit is task-dependent and follows from the smoothness of the physical basis: the networks represent smooth, continuously valued targets, including robotic kinematics, continuous control, and photovoltaic maximum-power-point tracking, with far fewer nodes and connections than multilayer perceptrons, but offer no parameter-efficiency advantage on classification-like decision boundaries. Trained networks transfer to hardware across approximately 35,000 connections with quantified fidelity, and a dedicated CMOS implementation is projected to operate at approximately 30 microwatts. A memristive realisation reproduces the same behaviour in simulation, indicating that the advantage comes from placing trainable nonlinearity on connections, rather than from a particular device.

Abstract: Extracting interpretable governing equations from sparse, noisy chemical time-series data remains difficult because discrete reaction topology and continuous kinetic parameters are tightly coupled. The methodological contribution is not a new MCMC or GP family in isolation; rather, it is the integration of these components into a physically constrained workflow with explicit uncertainty-aware acquisition choices. On the H2 + Br2 benchmark, the constrained sampler distinguishes elementary radical pathways from deceptive phenomenological fits in our experiments. On styrene epoxidation, the CIGP optimization loop improves final yield by 12.5% over the reported GP-BO baseline. A new 10-seed acquisition study shows that EI, GWU, PC-EI, uncertainty sampling, discrepancy hunting, and random search have different trade-offs: PC-EI substantially reduces low-yield BO suggestions, while EI-style criteria give the strongest final-yield performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出双重视角元学习框架MEDIC，通过联合域间和类间任务分裂的隐式梯度匹配，动态优化决策边界，实现对域和类的双重平衡。

Abstract: Domain generalization learns from multiple source domains to generalize to unseen target domains. However, it often neglects the realistic case of label mismatch between source and target. Open set domain generalization is then proposed to recognize unseen classes in unseen domains. A simple approach trains one-vs-all classifiers to separate each class and detect outliers as unknown. Yet, the imbalance between few positive samples and many negative samples skews the decision boundary towards the positive ones, leading the model to over-reject out-of-distribution data, even from known classes in unseen domains. In this paper, we propose a novel meta-learning stategy called dualistic MEta-learning with joint DomaIn-Class matching (MEDIC), which considers implicit gradient matching towards inter-domain and inter-class task splits simultaneously to find optimal boundaries balanced for both domains and classes. Experimental results show that MEDIC not only outperforms prior methods in open set scenarios, but also maintains competitive close set generalization ability.

### [191] [One Ruler: A Same-Hands Re-Evaluation of Bivariate Causal Direction on Tuebingen, with a Parameter-Free Compression Baseline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23767)
*Wietse Stienstra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新评估了Tuebingen因果对上的模型表现，指出以往研究因使用不同评估协议（如子集选择、权重、模型选择和决策率）导致结果不可比。作者采用统一标准（相同102对数据、无调参、强制决策）进行重测，引入零参数基线方法‘排序条件压缩’（基于bz2压缩），发现其在加权准确率达74.7%（p=3.7e-7），甚至在与SLOPE对比的100对上达76.0%，仅略低于其作者报告的77.2%（差异不显著）。原论文中被广泛引用的RECI 77.5%实为错误复制，正确值应为70.7%；而SLOPE的82.4%为选择性子集结果，真实可复现值为81.7%。所有方法在新标准下均集中在70-75%区间，且基线压缩法表现最强。文章揭示了夸大性能的机制（测试集调参、显著性筛选弃权），并提出压缩分数大小可作为模型无关的混淆信号（p=2.8e-68），以及预注册的虚假检验失败，限制了方法的理论解释力。代码、注册记录与每对输出均已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对Tuebingen因果对的评估缺乏一致性，不同研究使用各自独立的协议，导致结果不可比，可能误导对方法真实性能的理解。为获得公平比较，需要一个统一、严格的标准来重评现有方法。

Method: 采用相同102对因果数据，所有方法由作者统一运行，禁止超参数调优，强制每个样本做出决策。引入零参数基线‘排序条件压缩’：对量化、排序、一阶差分后的数据使用标准压缩器bz2。通过一致性评估框架，系统重测多种方法，并分析性能膨胀来源。

Result: 在统一评估下，多数方法表现集中在70%-75%之间，零参数压缩基线达到74.7%加权准确率，优于或接近多数复杂模型。原始文献中的高估结果多源于测试集调参和选择性报告（如只报告显著性测试通过的对）。压缩分数大小可有效标识潜在混淆因素（p=2.8e-68）。预注册的虚假检验失败，表明方法存在理论解释边界。

Conclusion: 当前因果推断方法在该数据集上的性能被严重高估，统一评估框架下，简单压缩基线已能与复杂模型竞争。研究强调评估协议的一致性与透明性的重要性，并建议未来工作采用标准化流程与公开输出以确保可复现性。

Abstract: Headline accuracies on the Tuebingen cause-effect pairs are routinely compared across papers even though each is measured under its authors' own protocol -- different pair subsets, weightings, model-selection, and decision rates. We argue this is the wrong comparison and run the right one: a same-hands re-evaluation in which every method is run by us on the identical 102 pairs, with one strict rule -- no tuning and a decision forced on every pair. As a clean reference point we introduce a deliberately minimal baseline: sorted-conditional compression, which feeds quantized, sorted, first-differenced data to an off-the-shelf compressor (bz2) and has zero fitted parameters. Under the common ruler the ranking differs sharply from the literature. Our baseline reaches 74.7% weighted accuracy (p = 3.7e-7); on the same 100 pairs that SLOPE is evaluated on it scores 76.0%, a 1.2-point gap below the authors' own forced-decision SLOPE (77.2%) that is well inside noise (McNemar p = 0.39). A faithful re-run of RECI lands at 70.7% -- inside the original authors' reported error bar, not the 77.5% often quoted (which we trace to a mis-copied cell). SLOPE's published 82.4% is a decided-subset figure: scoring the authors' own stored output only on the pairs its significance test chose to answer reproduces 81.7%. Under the common ruler the methods cluster in the low-to-mid 70s and the zero-parameter compressor ties the strongest of them. We document the mechanisms that inflate published figures (test-set model selection, significance-gated abstention) and contribute two further results: compression score magnitude is a model-free confounding flag (p = 2.8e-68), and a pre-registered falsification test fails in an instructive way that bounds the method's theoretical interpretation. Code, pre-registrations, and per-pair outputs are released.

Result: SurfBind achieves state-of-the-art performance on epitope prediction benchmarks, including SAbDab and DB5.5, and demonstrates robust generalization to unseen antibodies and conformational states.

Conclusion: Surface-centric modeling with interaction-aware design significantly enhances epitope prediction, offering new insights into protein-protein interactions and paving the way for more accurate antibody-antigen interface analysis.

Abstract: Molecular surfaces encode the geometric and physicochemical patterns that determine antibody-antigen recognition, central to epitope prediction. However, existing methods rely on sequences or backbone structures and struggle to capture discontinuous, surface-driven epitopes. This study presents SurfBind, a surface-centric learning framework for epitope prediction that operates directly on molecular surface representations. Experiments on challenging epitope identification benchmarks, including SAbDab and DB5.5, demonstrate that SurfBind achieves state-of-the-art performance and strong generalization across unseen antibodies and conformational states, highlighting the value of interaction-aware surface modeling for understanding the crucial mechanisms of protein-protein interactions.

### [193] [Reconstructing GRACE Terrestrial Water Storage with Spatio-Temporal Graph Neural Networks: An Application to South America](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23833)
*Lukas Arzoumanidis,Lara Johannsen,Klara Middendorf,Annette Eicker,Youness Dehbi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于多变量时间序列图神经网络（MTGNN）的深度学习方法，重建自1940年以来的月度GRACE类陆地水储量异常（TWSA），利用ERA5气象强迫数据与GRACE观测之间的关系。相比传统网格逐点回归或LSTM等方法，新模型通过静态可解释的混合邻接矩阵捕捉空间依赖性，结合地理距离与气候时间序列滞后相关性，有效建模局部水文耦合与大尺度遥相关。重建结果在网格单元上达到0.69的皮尔逊相关系数，流域平均达0.94，偏差接近零，并成功再现2015/16厄尔尼诺和2020/21拉尼娜事件的空间指纹。与现有重建方法（GTWS-MLrec、RM-REC、GRAiCE）对比显示，本模型在流域尺度上统计性能相当，且仅需其1/2至1/10的输入变量，在干旱地区仍存在共性弱点。代码已公开于GitHub。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRACE和GRACE-FO卫星提供的陆地水储量变化观测记录从2002年开始，时间跨度较短，难以支持长期气候尺度分析。因此需要一种可靠的方法重建更早时期的陆地水储量异常（TWSA），以揭示气候变化与人类活动对全球水循环的影响。

Method: 采用多变量时间序列图神经网络（MTGNN）架构，结合每日ERA5气象数据（降水、蒸散发、径流）与月度GRACE观测，通过构建一个融合地理距离与气候时间序列滞后相关性的静态混合邻接矩阵，捕捉空间依赖关系，实现从1940年至今的月度TWSA重建。

Result: 重建结果在网格单元上获得0.69的皮尔逊相关系数，流域平均相关系数达0.94，偏差接近零；能准确再现2015/16厄尔尼诺和2020/21拉尼娜事件的空间特征。在与主流重建方法比较中，本模型在流域尺度表现相当，但所需预测因子数量仅为其他模型的1/2至1/10，且在干旱地区存在普遍性弱点。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于图神经网络的TWSA重建方法具有高精度、低输入复杂度和良好的物理可解释性，为长期水文变化研究提供了有力工具，尤其适用于气候尺度分析。代码已开源，便于复现与扩展。

Abstract: Terrestrial water storage (TWS) integrates snow, soil moisture, surface water, and groundwater and is a key indicator of how climate variability and human activity reshape the global water cycle. The GRACE and GRACE-FO satellite missions provide the only direct, globally consistent observations of TWS change, but their record only begins in 2002 which is too short for many climate-scale analyses. We present a deep learning application that reconstructs monthly GRACE-like TWS anomalies (TWSA) back to 1940 by learning the relationship between daily ERA5 meteorological forcing (precipitation, evapotranspiration, runoff) and monthly GRACE observations. In contrast to prior reconstruction approaches based on grid-cell-wise regression, CNNs, or LSTMs, we adapt a multi-variate time series graph neural network (MTGNN) architecture, which was originally developed for mobility and traffic forecasting on urban sensor networks to this satellite-geodesy task. Spatial dependencies are encoded in a static, interpretable hybrid adjacency matrix that combines geodesic proximity with lagged correlations of climatic time series, capturing both local hydrological coupling and large-scale teleconnections. The reconstruction achieves a grid-cell Pearson correlation of 0.69, a basin-mean correlation of 0.94, and a near-zero bias, and it reproduces the spatial fingerprints of the 2015/16 El Niño and 2020/21 La Niña events. A systematic comparison with established reconstruction approaches (GTWS-MLrec, RM-REC, GRAiCE) shows that the graph-based model is statistically competitive at basin scale, reaching a correlation within 0.025 of the best baseline while using only roughly half to a tenth of the predictors the other models require and revealing characteristic weaknesses in arid regions in all models. The complete implementation is publicly available at github.com/hcu-cml/MTGNN-TWS-Reconstruction-GRACE

### [194] [The Degeneracy Distillery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23838)
*T. Lucas Makinen,Deaglan J. Bartlett,Niall Jeffrey,Benjamin D. Wandelt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为"退化精炼器"的方法，能够自动且符号化地从参数-数据对中检测并解决参数组合的退化问题。该方法通过估计和展平费舍尔信息矩阵来探索似然的信息几何，将退化视为物理模型的内在属性，无需实际观测数据。在合成与真实世界问题中，该方法发现了能产生独立数据影响的参数组合的符号坐标变换，全局性地展平费舍尔信息，显著减少下游神经后验估计所需的模拟预算，最多可减少10倍模拟量，同时提供物理系统洞察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当多个参数或标签产生相似数据时，会导致退化，使标签预测和反问题求解困难，因为机器学习算法和概率采样器依赖于数据及其梯度的可区分性。识别物理模型或真实数据中的退化有助于理解模型选择或数据生成过程。现有方法通常局限于单点展平，缺乏全局性，且难以提供符号解释。因此需要一种能自动、符号化地检测并解决退化问题的方法。

Method: 提出退化精炼器，基于参数-数据（或参数-仿真）对，通过估计和展平费舍尔信息矩阵，探索似然函数的信息几何结构。利用信息几何分析，将退化视为模型的内在属性，不依赖实际观测数据。通过寻找符号坐标变换，使得新坐标下参数对数据的影响独立，从而实现全局展平费舍尔信息。

Result: 在多种合成与真实世界问题上验证了该方法的有效性。发现的符号坐标变换能够识别出对数据有独立影响的参数组合，实现全局展平费舍尔信息。相比传统基于后验的展平方法，该方法在保持验证校准精度的前提下，模拟次数最多减少10倍，并提供了对系统的物理洞察。

Conclusion: 退化精炼器是一种有效的工具，能够自动、符号化地揭示和解决参数退化问题，不仅提升了下游后验估计的效率，还增强了对模型内在结构的理解，为复杂系统建模与数据分析提供了新的视角。

Abstract: When two or more parameters or labels produce similar data, they are degenerate, or hard to distinguish. Degeneracies render both label prediction and inverse problems difficult, since both machine learning algorithms and probabilistic samplers rely on the distinguishability of data and its gradients with respect to parameters. However, identifying degeneracies in physical models or real-world datasets can be elucidating about the choice of model or the underlying process that produces the data. We present the degeneracy distillery, a method that (1) detects and (2) resolves degenerate parameter combinations (a) automatically and (b) symbolically, from parameter-data (or parameter-simulation) pairs alone, through estimation and flattening of the Fisher information matrix. By exploring the information geometry of the likelihood, we characterize degeneracies as an intrinsic property of the physical model, requiring no realised data observation. We demonstrate our approach on a range of synthetic and real-world problems, discovering symbolic coordinate transformations that identify the combinations of parameters of a model which yield independent effects on the data. The resulting coordinates flatten the Fisher information in expectation globally, in contrast to posterior-based methods that flatten only at a single point, and substantially reduce the simulation budget required for downstream neural posterior estimation. In test cases we require up to $10\times$ fewer simulations for posterior estimation at matched validation calibration whilst simultaneously gaining physical insight on the system.

</details>


### [195] [Machine Learning Modeling for Real-Time Melt Pool Monitoring in Laser Powder Bed Fusion Additive Manufacturing: A Hybrid Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23851)
*Inioluwa Emmanuel,Zhuo Yang,Ho Yeung,Xinyao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于深度学习与传统机器学习结合的二值图像分类框架，用于激光粉末床熔融（LPBF）增材制造中的实时熔池异常检测。采用1,200张镍基超合金625的熔池图像构建平衡数据集，评估了ResNet50、EfficientNetB0、MobileNetV2三种迁移学习模型及两种随机森林方法（基于特征嵌入与原始像素）在准确率、推理时间、资源消耗等方面的性能。结果显示，混合型EfficientNetB0+随机森林模型在测试集上达到F1分数0.9451、准确率0.9458、AUC 0.9904，且单图推理时间仅1.15毫秒，显著优于纯深度学习模型。该方法在数据有限条件下实现了高精度与低延迟，具备工厂部署可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现增材制造中熔池状态的实时监控对保障零件质量至关重要。然而，真实生产环境中高质量标注数据稀缺，且对计算资源和响应速度有严格要求，亟需高效、鲁棒的异常检测方法。

Result: 混合型EfficientNetB0+随机森林模型表现最优：测试集上F1得分0.9451，准确率0.9458，AUC达0.9904，单图推理延迟仅为1.15毫秒；纯深度学习模型虽精度尚可但推理耗时显著更高；整体表明融合预训练特征与经典集成学习的方法在精度与效率之间取得良好平衡。

Conclusion: 在数据受限的增材制造场景下，将预训练卷积神经网络提取的特征与随机森林等传统机器学习方法相结合，是一种兼具高精度、低延迟与强部署适应性的有效策略，适用于工厂级实时熔池异常监测系统。

Abstract: This work investigates the implementation of artificial intelligence and machine learning (AI/ML) for real-time monitoring in laser powder bed fusion (LPBF) additive manufacturing. We developed a binary image classification framework for distinguishing normal and abnormal melt pool images using a balanced dataset of 1,200 images collected from Nickel superalloy 625 on the NIST AMMT platform. The study evaluates accuracy and inference time based on control requirements and hardware limitations of open-architecture LPBF machines. We benchmark three transfer learning architectures (ResNet50, EfficientNetB0, and MobileNetV2) against two Random Forest approaches: one trained on EfficientNetB0 feature embeddings (hybrid) and one trained on raw pixel features (baseline). Images are stratified into 80/20 train-test splits, with a further 90/10 validation split on the training set, and undergo standardized resizing, normalization, and label-preserving data augmentation to emulate realistic process variability. Each model is evaluated using accuracy, precision, recall, F1 score, and area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC), along with training time, inference latency, and CPU & GPU usage to capture deployability constraints relevant to factory-floor monitoring. The hybrid EfficientNetB0-plus-Random Forest approach achieves the best performance on the held-out test set, with an F1 score of 0.9451, accuracy of 0.9458, and AUC of 0.9904, while maintaining sub-millisecond per-image inference (1.15 ms). In contrast, purely deep learning models exhibit significantly higher inference times with lower accuracy. These results demonstrate that combining pre-trained convolutional features with classical ensemble methods provides a robust, computationally efficient route to real-time melt pool anomaly detection in data-limited additive manufacturing environments.

Result: Sesame在多个基准测试中表现出色，不仅可实现高质量的从头分子生成，还能有效根据给定骨架或片段进行合理扩展，支持高效的先导优化流程。实验表明其生成结果在化学合理性、多样性及与靶点结合能力方面均优于现有方法。

Incorporating each feature poses a critical challenge. Equally important, yet often treated as secondary, is the ability to grow a molecule from a partial starting point -- a scaffold or fragment supplied by a chemist -- which is the central operation of lead optimization. We present Sesame (Spatial Evoformer for a Structure-Aware Molecular Engine), a diffusion-based molecular generation model that leverages a novel spatial pairformer module to condition on partial molecular structure and the surrounding protein pocket, both expressed as continuous spatial density maps. In addition to this module, we also introduce a diffusion framework for joint denoising of atom types, bond types, and positions, along with a trajectory finetuning scheme that trains on the model's own sampling rollouts to improve generation quality. Sesame is trained on a large corpus of ligand-only and protein-ligand datasets.

### [197] [Are Safety Guarantees in Neural Networks Safe? How to Compute Trustworthy Robustness Certifications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23858)
*Merkouris Papamichail,Konstantinos Varsos,Giorgos Flouris,João Marques-Silva*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的鲁棒性认证方法，通过引入‘边心距’（apothem）度量，实现了在合理计算开销下对神经网络鲁棒性的有效评估。相较于传统以体积最大化为目标的方法，该方法在时间复杂度上具有显著优势，并证明了基于查询的体积最优认证算法在理论上不可行。此外，作者提出了双认证机制，提供更紧致的上界估计。实验表明，所提出的ParallelepipedoNN系统在MNIST和Fashion MNIST数据集上相较现有方法在最小边长上提升至少两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有鲁棒性认证方法主要追求最大体积，但受制于计算复杂性，无法在合理时间内实现体积最优。因此需要寻找新的优化目标与高效算法，以兼顾认证质量与计算效率。

Method: 提出边心距（apothem）作为新的优化指标，设计基于神经网络验证器（oracle）的线性次数调用算法来计算边心距最优认证；引入双认证机制，构建包含所有同类样本的区间，用于提供更紧的上界。

Result: 所提方法可在输入域直径的线性次数调用验证器的情况下完成边心距最优认证；理论证明体积最优认证在基于查询的框架下不可实现；实验显示在标准数据集上最小边长性能优于现有方法至少两倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出的边心距最优认证方法在计算效率与认证质量之间取得了良好平衡，且其双认证机制提供了更强的理论保证，为实际部署中的安全推理提供了新思路。

Abstract: A primary challenge in AI safety is the existence of adversarial examples -- slightly distorted inputs that cause a neural network (NN) to misclassify. To mitigate this problem, recent research focuses on the computation of robustness certifications, which, for a given input, determine the largest distortion the input may receive without breaking the network's prediction. Robustness certifications can be interpreted as an axis-aligned hyper-rectangle (multi-dimensional intervals). Most existing approaches focus on maximizing the certification's volume, but recent intractability results prohibit the computation of volume-optimal certifications in reasonable time. We introduce the apothem measure and show how to compute apothem-optimal certifications in a linear number of calls to a NN verifier (oracle) w.r.t. the input domain's diameter. Moreover, we prove that we cannot have a volume-optimal, oracle-based algorithm, even if we discard the oracle costs. Also, we introduce dual certifications -- an interval including all instances of a class -- thus providing apothem-minimum upper bounds to a robustness certification. Further, we present the ParallelepipedoNN system, which we evaluate on the standard MNIST and Fashion MNIST benchmarks. A preliminary comparison with existing work on the same datasets reveals at least two-fold improvement w.r.t. the minimum edge length.

</details>


### [198] [Exact Schur-Sylvester Dimensionality Reductions for Non-Smooth Stochastic Complexity and Manifold Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23867)
*Trenton Lau,Gary P. T. Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数学上等价的精确计算方法，解决了正则非光滑估计器（如Lasso）在计算归一化最大似然（NML）码长时因流形约束投影和体积积分导致的立方级计算瓶颈问题。通过引入分块舒尔补和西尔维斯特行列式恒等式，将每步计算复杂度从$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$降低至$\mathcal{O}(k^3 + N^2 k)$，并推广到稀疏支持向量机、弹性网和组Lasso。实验表明，在高维数据上实现了超过14,100倍的加速，且保持双精度数值等价性，使大规模统计推断中的精确非光滑NML估计成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在计算非光滑模型的NML码长时面临严重的计算瓶颈，主要源于流形约束投影和体积积分的高复杂度，限制了其在大规模数据上的应用。因此需要一种高效且精确的替代方案。

Method: 利用分块舒尔补和西尔维斯特行列式恒等式，重构投影算子与体积因子的计算方式，从而避免高复杂度的矩阵求逆与行列式计算。

Result: 计算复杂度从$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$降至$\mathcal{O}(k^3 + N^2 k)$，实测速度提升超过14,100倍，同时保持双精度数值等价性，验证了方法在高维数据上的高效性和稳定性。

Conclusion: 该方法成功突破了非光滑模型中NML计算的性能瓶颈，为大规模统计推断提供了高效、精确的工具，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: The exact computation of the Normalized Maximum Likelihood (NML) codelength for regular non-smooth estimators (e.g., Lasso) has been historically limited by the cubic scaling walls of manifold-constrained projection and volume integration. At each step of the geometric Propose-and-Project Metropolis--Hastings (PPMH) sampler, evaluating the projection operator requires inverting an $(N+k) \times (N+k)$ generalized KKT matrix, while calculating the volume factor requires the determinant of an $(N-k) \times (N-k)$ Gram matrix. This paper presents an exact, mathematically equivalent formulation that bypasses both bottlenecks by utilizing the block Schur complement and Sylvester's determinant identity. We prove that the computational complexity of both operations collapses from $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$ to $\mathcal{O}(k^3 + N^2 k)$ per step. We generalize this reduction to Sparse Support Vector Machines (SVMs), Elastic Net, and Group Lasso. Finally, we provide a rigorous numerical stability analysis and evaluate the sampler's efficiency using the Effective Sample Size (ESS) per second. Our empirical benchmarks on high-dimensional datasets confirm a constant speedup exceeding $14{,}100\times$ while maintaining double-precision numerical equivalence, rendering exact non-smooth NML estimation highly tractable for large-scale statistical inference.

### [199] [Federated Survival Analysis in Healthcare: A Multi-Model Evaluation on Cross-Institutional Heterogeneous Breast Cancer Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23871)
*Natalia Moreno-Blasco,Anusha Ihalapathirana,Pekka Siirtola,Miguel Fernandez-de-Retana*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 联邦学习在大多数情况下优于本地训练，部分场景下性能接近甚至超过集中式训练；随机生存森林（RSF）在各项性能指标上表现最优，具备良好的平衡性；客户端分布多样性显著影响模型性能；FedAvg和FedProx在稳定性与性能上优于FedAdam。

Abstract: Survival analysis is central to clinical decision-making, yet reliable time-to-event models require large, diverse cohorts that are rarely available at a single institution, while privacy regulations restrict the centralization of patient data. Federated learning (FL) offers a privacy-preserving alternative by training shared models without exchanging raw data, but its effectiveness for survival modeling under realistic, heterogeneous conditions remains insufficiently understood. This paper presents a systematic, multi-model evaluation of federated survival analysis on a cross-institutional breast cancer cohort with naturally heterogeneous distributed clients. Three representative survival models, the Cox Proportional Hazards model, DeepSurv, and Random Survival Forest (RSF), are compared across centralized, local, and federated training, and three federated optimization strategies (FedAvg, FedProx, and FedAdam) are assessed for the gradient-based models. Results show that FL consistently outperforms local training and approaches, and occasionally exceeds, centralized performance, while RSF offers the best overall balance of discrimination, calibration, and robustness across heterogeneous clients. We further find that performance depends on the diversity of client distributions, and that FedAvg and FedProx are stronger and more stable than FedAdam. ### [200] [MGI: Member vs Generated Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23872)
*Bihe Zhao,Michel Meintz,Juangui Xu,Franziska Boenisch,Adam Dziedzic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为Data Circuit Breaker (DCB)的新方法，用于解决生成模型中难以区分训练数据与生成样本的挑战（即成员 vs 生成推理，MGI）。现有方法在处理此类问题时存在系统性误判：基于似然的方法将生成样本错误分类为训练成员，而基于归属的方法则常将真实训练样本误判为生成内容。这是因为两者均依赖于相似的高似然信号。DCB通过结合自编码器和潜在生成器的互补信号，在多类图像生成模型（如自回归和扩散模型）上表现出色，有效克服了现有方法的局限性，并在处理近似重复样本及衍生模型场景下仍保持鲁棒性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成模型生成的内容越来越接近人类创作，难以判断某数据点是来自原始训练集还是由模型生成。特别是当模型记忆并再现训练数据时，这一问题更加突出。现有的成员推理和归属方法在实际应用中存在系统性偏差，无法可靠区分真实训练样本与生成样本，因此需要一种更稳健、更准确的区分机制。

Method: 提出Data Circuit Breaker (DCB)，一个三阶段框架，融合生成模型的自编码器与潜在生成器提供的互补信号。第一阶段利用自编码器提取输入样本的重构误差特征；第二阶段分析潜在空间中的生成一致性；第三阶段结合两者信号进行最终分类决策。该方法不依赖单一的似然信号，从而避免了传统方法的缺陷。

Result: DCB在多种主流生成模型（包括图像自回归模型和扩散模型）上均表现优异，显著优于现有成员推理和归属方法。即使面对模型复制近似训练样本的情况，仍能准确区分。此外，其在新模型基于生成数据训练的复杂场景下也展现出良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: Data Circuit Breaker (DCB) 提供了一种有效且通用的解决方案来应对生成模型中的成员与生成样本混淆问题。通过整合多源信号，避免了对似然信号的依赖，显著提升了分类准确性与鲁棒性，为保障数据隐私和模型可信性提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: As generative models increasingly produce samples that are indistinguishable from human-created content, it becomes difficult to determine whether a given data point was part of a model's natural training set or was generated by the model itself, especially when models memorize and reproduce training data. We formalize this challenge as Member vs Generated Inference (MGI): given a sample and a target generative model, infer whether the sample is a true training member or a generated output of that model. Focusing on image generation, we show that existing membership inference methods systematically misclassify generated samples as training members, while attribution-based methods often misclassify true members as generated. This failure arises because both approaches rely on likelihood-related signals that are similarly elevated for training examples and for the model's own outputs. To address MGI, we propose Data Circuit Breaker (DCB), a three-stage method that combines complementary signals from a generative model's autoencoder and latent generator to distinguish training members from generated samples. Across multiple generative models, including image autoregressive and diffusion models, DCB consistently addresses the shortcomings of membership inference and attribution methods, remains effective even when models reproduce near-duplicates of training samples, and generalizes to challenging model derivative settings in which new models are trained on generated data.

</details>


### [201] [GRACE: Gated Refinement for Accurate Causal Edge Discovery in High-Dimensional Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23880)
*Mohammad Fesanghary,Abhinav Havaldar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRACE 是一种用于高维时间序列中准确因果边发现的新方法，通过使用带有 $L_0$ 正则化的 Hard Concrete 门来精炼约束基础发现。该方法在保持高精度的同时显著提升 F1 得分，并在合成与真实数据上均优于现有方法，尤其在计算效率上远超传统非线性条件独立测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代时间序列数据通常包含数十甚至上百个相互作用的变量，导致因果发现极具挑战性。现有的约束基方法在非线性条件独立检验方面难以扩展，而评分基方法则依赖于任意阈值来二值化连续边得分，缺乏鲁棒性。因此需要一种既能保证统计严谨性又可高效处理大规模数据的因果发现方法。

Method: GRACE 利用 Hard Concrete 门结合 $L_0$ 正则化，为每个候选边分配一个独立的门控变量，使其值集中在 0 或 1，实现清晰的二元分离。首先通过快速线性条件独立检验获取高召回率的初始骨架，再用单一门控模型学习哪些边能真正提升预测性能，自动适应问题维度和骨架密度进行正则化，从而有效剔除假阳性。

Result: 在多种拓扑结构（如尺度无关、Erdős-Rényi、小世界）和高达 $d=100$ 维度的合成基准测试中，GRACE 显著提升了基础 CI 方法的 F1 得分，同时保持高精度；相比注意力机制和评分基方法表现更优。在真实河流流量数据上，其时间自举变体成功识别出 Elbe 河流 9/11 条因果边，仅 1 个误报（F1=0.86，AUROC=0.99），将原始骨架中的 106 个误报减少 99%。整体速度比昂贵的非线性 CI 测试快 75 倍。

Conclusion: GRACE 通过门控精炼机制实现了高精度、高效率且可扩展的因果发现，在复杂现实场景下表现出色，是当前大规模因果推断的重要进展。

Abstract: From climate teleconnections to gene regulation, modern time-series datasets encompass tens or hundreds of interacting variables, making causal discovery increasingly challenging. Constraint-based methods offer statistical rigor but their nonlinear CI tests are infeasible at scale, while score-based alternatives avoid CI testing but require arbitrary thresholds to binarize continuous edge scores. We propose GRACE ($\textbf{G}$ated $\textbf{R}$efinement for $\textbf{A}$ccurate $\textbf{C}$ausal $\textbf{E}$dge discovery), which refines constraint-based discovery using Hard Concrete gates with $L_0$ regularization: each candidate edge has an independent gate whose values concentrate near 0 or 1, yielding a clean bimodal separation that makes the binary decision robust, unlike the narrow, overlapping score distributions produced by $L_1$ and attention-based methods. A fast linear CI skeleton provides high-recall candidates; a single gated model then prunes false positives by learning which edges genuinely improve prediction, with automatic regularization adapted to problem dimensions and skeleton density. Systematic experiments on synthetic benchmarks, spanning diverse graph topologies (scale-free, Erdős-R'enyi, small-world) and dimensionalities up to $d=100$, show that GRACE substantially improves F1 over its base CI method while maintaining high precision, and outperforms attention-based and score-based alternatives. GRACE matches or exceeds expensive nonlinear CI tests at a fraction of the cost ($75\times$ faster). On a real-world river flow dataset, where rainfall confounders, variable propagation lags, and distributional shifts violate standard assumptions, a temporal bootstrap variant of GRACE recovers 9 of 11 causal edges along the Elbe River with only 1 false positive ($F_1 = 0.86$, AUROC${} = 0.99$), reducing the skeleton's 106 false positives by 99%.

### [202] [ARIA: Adaptive Region-Based Importance Allocation for Conditional Diffusion Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23898)
*Loay Mualem,Vinh Tong,Samir Darouich,Mathias Niepert*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ARIA 是一种自适应分配训练资源的框架，用于条件扩散模型的知识蒸馏。它通过在线估计教师-学生在不同条件区域的差异，将训练重点放在对齐不佳的区域，从而提升蒸馏效果，尤其在未见和低频条件下表现更优。理论分析表明，在有界方差和漂移假设下，该机制能有效追踪训练过程中的动态偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 条件扩散模型知识蒸馏面临的主要挑战是难以将知识泛化到训练分布之外，因为预测噪声强烈依赖于条件信号。现有方法虽通过切换条件扩大条件空间，但缺乏对训练资源的高效分配策略，导致在大量条件中无法有效利用有限计算资源。

Method: ARIA 采用基于区域的自适应训练策略，将条件空间划分为粗粒度区域，实时监控每个区域的教师-学生差异，并根据差异大小动态调整训练权重，确保重点优化对齐较差的区域，同时保持原始蒸馏目标不变。

Result: 实验表明，ARIA 在大多数架构和设置下优于现有方法（如 RC），特别是在未见条件和低频条件场景中提升显著；理论分析验证了其在有界方差与漂移条件下能够稳定追踪训练过程中的误差演化。

Conclusion: ARIA 提供了一种高效、可扩展的条件扩散模型知识蒸馏方案，通过自适应资源分配显著提升泛化能力，尤其适用于大规模、多样化的条件空间。

Abstract: Distilling conditional diffusion models aims to transfer the behavior of a large teacher to a smaller student while preserving alignment across conditioning inputs. Unlike recognition tasks, knowledge distillation in conditional diffusion often struggles to transfer knowledge beyond the training distribution, since the predicted noise strongly depends on the conditioning signal. As a result, effective distillation requires exploring a large conditioning space. In practical settings, this creates a major bottleneck. Paired image-condition data may be limited, and generating synthetic images for every available condition is often computationally infeasible, while the pool of conditions, such as text prompts, can be extremely large. Recent work addresses this issue by switching conditions during training, exposing the student to a broader conditioning space without changing the distillation objective. Yet this raises a complementary question: once a large conditioning corpus is available, how should the training effort be allocated? In this work, we introduce ARIA, a framework that adaptively allocates training effort across coarse regions of the conditioning space. By maintaining online estimates of teacher-student discrepancy at the region level, ARIA focuses updates where misalignment persists while preserving the original distillation objective. Empirically, ARIA improves over RC across most architectures and settings, with the clearest gains observed in unseen and underrepresented regimes. We also provide a theoretical analysis showing that the proposed tracking mechanism follows the evolving discrepancy during training under bounded variance and drift assumptions.

Result: 在德国程序期限计算、美国宪法商业条款分析以及跨司法管辖区制裁比例性三个真实法律任务上均成功应用该架构，实现了高可靠性的法律推理输出。同时，该架构为法律AI训练提供了确定性的外部验证机制，填补了强化学习在法律领域中的反馈空白。

Conclusion: 所提出的架构不仅提升了法律AI在形式化任务中的正确性，还在开放性法律推理中提供了结构性保障，具备广泛适用性，并为法律AI的可信训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: This article develops an architecture that creates a formally verifiable reward signal to train legal AI, adapting the LLM proposes, verifier disposes paradigm from mathematical AI to the distinctive demands of law. We present an architecture comprising LLM-driven autoformalization into a formal legal calculus extending Catala, a verification kernel, and explanation generation grounded in formal proof traces. For the computational components of law, the architecture provides provable correctness. For open-textured legal analysis, it provides structural guarantees: every required stage of the legal argument is addressed, argumentation is exercised at the correct stages and not omitted, and the deductive links between steps are valid. We demonstrate the architecture on procedural deadline calculations in German law, Commerce Clause analysis in U.S. constitutional law, and cross-jurisdictional sanction proportionality. We further show that the same architecture has a structural advantage for legal AI training: a deterministic external verifier supplies verifiable outcomes for legal problems and thereby closes the traditional reinforcement-learning loop gap in law.

In this work, we argue that this task is often infeasible for vanilla conditional diffusion models: we conjecture that no inference-time technique can efficiently produce samples from the target distribution in certain well-motivated settings. This idea is supported by theory-guided generalization arguments and carefully-designed experiments on both synthetic and realistic data. In particular, while recent methods such as Feynman-Kac correction reduce inference-time approximation error, our results show that score estimation error has a more catastrophic effect on performance when the target distribution is out-of-distribution with respect to the sources, highlighting the need for a different approach to this task.

### [205] [KLip-PPO: A per-sample KL perspective on PPO-Clip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23932)
*Riccardo Colletti,Robin Holzinger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了PPO中裁剪代理损失与KL惩罚损失之间的内在等价性，表明前者可通过一个随样本变化的KL代理损失精确复现，且该系数具有显式表达式。这一发现统一了两种形式的PPO，并揭示了裁剪策略中隐含的分段常数惩罚结构，为算法改进提供了新的设计视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献将PPO的两种形式（裁剪代理与KL惩罚）视为独立算法，分别处理其梯度、超参数和实现，导致大量经验比较。然而，这两种形式在理论上是否存在等价性尚不明确，亟需澄清其内在联系以推动算法理解与改进。

Method: 通过数学推导证明：裁剪代理损失的梯度可被一个系数随样本变化的KL代理损失完全复现，该系数依赖于重要性比率和优势值，且该等价关系在每个小批量步骤和整个内循环中均成立。

Result: 在五个MuJoCo连续控制基准测试中，基于两种损失的训练曲线几乎无法区分，验证了理论等价性；同时揭示了裁剪策略中隐含的分段常数惩罚机制，即在信任区域边界处呈现阶跃函数形式。

Conclusion: PPO-Clip的裁剪机制本质上是一种随样本变化的非线性KL惩罚，其系数形状是算法泛化的自然设计轴。这一发现为后续改进PPO提供了理论基础和方向。

Abstract: Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) is the standard policy-gradient algorithm for on-policy reinforcement learning. The literature presents it in two forms, a clipped surrogate that bounds the importance ratio between successive policies and a Kullback-Leibler penalty between them. These forms are treated as separate algorithms with their own gradients, their own hyperparameters, and their own reference implementations, and a sizeable body of empirical work compares them. We show that the gradient of the clipped surrogate is reproduced exactly by a Kullback-Leibler surrogate whose coefficient varies per sample, with closed-form dependence on the importance ratio and the advantage. The identity holds at every minibatch step and across the entire inner loop, and on five MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks the two losses produce indistinguishable training curves. The reformulation exposes a structural feature of the clipped surrogate that the min notation hides. PPO-Clip's implicit per-sample penalty is a step function at the boundary of the trust region, and the shape of this coefficient is the natural design axis for generalising the algorithm. We sketch the resulting follow-up directions in the discussion.

### [206] [DREG: A Layer-Wise Jacobian Regularization as a General-Purpose Penalty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23942)
*Rowan Martnishn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过960次实验的全面实证分析，评估了导数正则化（DREG）的性能。结果显示，DREG在整体准确率和干净数据场景下表现最佳，显著优于无正则化、权重衰减和IGPen等方法；在噪声鲁棒性上仅次于谱归一化（SN），是少数层间正则化方法之一。DREG在GELU激活函数下表现尤为突出，尤其适用于现代视觉与自然语言处理任务。其优势在数据稀缺时最明显，表明其作为几何归纳偏置可替代数据量带来的正则效果。整个实验中仅使用单一固定超参数λ=10⁻²·⁵，无需针对不同数据集调参，验证了其即插即用的实用性。这些发现与DREG设计一致：将正则化压力集中于激活导数较大的层，而非均匀约束网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究导数正则化（DREG）在不同条件下的有效性，明确其何时、何地以及为何起作用，并评估其在现代深度学习架构中的适用性与普适性。

Method: 进行全因子交叉实验，覆盖4种激活函数、6种正则化方法、8个数据集和5个随机种子，共960次实验，系统比较DREG与其他正则化方法的表现。所有实验均采用固定超参数λ=10⁻²·⁵，不进行数据集特定调优。

Result: DREG在整体准确率和干净数据场景下显著优于其他正则化方法（Wilcoxon p ≤ 0.031）；在噪声鲁棒性上仅次于谱归一化（SN）；在GELU激活下表现最优，尤其适用于视觉与自然语言处理任务；在数据稀缺条件下优势更明显；且仅需单一固定超参数即可有效应用。

Conclusion: DREG是一种高效、通用且即插即用的正则化方法，特别适合具有非平凡雅可比结构的神经网络，在数据有限或前沿深度学习任务中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We present a large-scale empirical study isolating the contributions of the Derivative Regularization penalty (DREG). Across a fully-crossed factorial sweep of 960 experiments spanning 4 activations, 6 regularizers, 8 datasets, and 5 random seeds, we ask: when, where, and why does DREG work? Our results establish three principal findings. First, DREG achieves the highest overall and clean-regime accuracy among all regularizers evaluated (significantly so against the unregularized baseline, Weight Decay, and IGPen; Wilcoxon $p \leq 0.031$). It ranks second in noise robustness behind Spectral Normalization (SN) - the only two layer-wise regularizers in the study. Second, DREG is globally the best-performing regularizer under GELU, the default activation in modern transformer architectures, particularly on both messy vision and messy NLP benchmarks, suggesting direct applicability to frontier deep learning settings. Third, DREG's advantage over competing regularizers is most pronounced under data scarcity, consistent with its role as a geometric inductive bias that substitutes for the regularizing effect of data volume. Throughout, DREG is applied with a single fixed hyperparameter $λ= 10^{-2.5}$ and no per-dataset tuning, supporting its characterization as a plug-and-play regularizer for neural networks with nontrivial Jacobian structure. These findings are consistent with DREG's design: concentrating regularization pressure on layers where the activation derivative is largest, rather than constraining the network uniformly.

### [207] [Learning the Koopman Operator using Attention Free Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23957)
*Mohammed Nagdi,Evangelos-Marios Nikolados,Alexey Yermakov,Mars Gao,Nathan Kutz,Filippo Menolascina*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于自编码器的Koopman学习方法在长期滚动预测中常因系统非线性、切换行为或强瞬态导致潜在空间漂移，引发相位与幅度误差，亟需增强对潜在流形的保持能力。

Method: 提出两种互补技术：(1) 注意力自由潜在记忆（AFT）块，通过滑动窗口聚合历史潜在状态生成修正后的潜在表示，用于后续Koopman更新；(2) 动态重编码机制，采用轻量级在线变化点检测算法（如EWMA、CUSUM、两样本检验）实时监测潜在空间漂移，并将预测结果投影回自编码器流形。

Result: 在多个基准系统（Duffing振子、Repressilator、IRMA）上，所提方法在长达1000步的预测中显著降低误差累积，优于标准Koopman自编码器、匹配容量的多头注意力模型、GRU与Transformer自编码器。同时具备更低推理延迟，实现高效且稳定的长期预测。

Conclusion: 结合AFT与动态重编码的Koopman预测框架，在保持低计算开销的同时，有效抑制了长期预测中的误差发散，实现了对复杂动力系统的高精度、长时间稳定建模，为实际应用提供了轻量级、鲁棒性强的解决方案。

Abstract: Learning Koopman operators with autoencoders enables linear prediction in a latent space, but long-horizon rollouts often drift off the learned manifold, leading to phase and amplitude errors on systems with switching, continuous spectra, or strong transients. We introduce two complementary components that make Koopman predictors more robust. First, we add an attention-free latent memory (AFT) block that aggregates a short window of past latents to produce a corrected latent before each Koopman update. Unlike multi-head attention, AFT operates in linear time and adds only $\approx$30k parameters ($3d^2 + T^2$, fewer than matched multi-head attention), yet captures the local temporal context needed to suppress error divergence. Second, we propose dynamic re-encoding: lightweight, online change-point triggers (EWMA, CUSUM, and sequential two-sample tests) that detect latent drift and project predictions back onto the autoencoder manifold. Across three benchmark systems -- Duffing oscillator, Repressilator, IRMA -- our model consistently reduces error accumulation compared to a Koopman autoencoder and matched-capacity multi-head attention. We also compare against GRU and Transformer autoencoders, evaluated both from initial conditions and with a 50-step context, and find that Koopman+AFT (with optional re-encoding) attains markedly lower long-horizon error while maintaining lower inference latency. We report improvements over horizons up to 1000 steps, together with ablations over trigger policies. The result is a fast, compact predictor that stays on the learned manifold over long horizons.

### [208] [Forget Without Compromise: Nexus Sampling for Streaming KV-Cache Eviction Under Fixed Budgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23961)
*Duc Duong,Hoang Anh Duy Le,Jianwen Xie,Anshumali Shrivastava,Zhaozhuo Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Nexus Sampling 是一种无需训练的缓存淘汰方法，通过迭代式注意力评分（Nexus scoring）识别关键桥接令牌，并结合加权水库采样保留重要信息，有效提升长上下文任务中微妙重要令牌的留存率。在80%缓存淘汰率下，其性能接近密集注意力，且在检索密集型任务上优于传统 top-K 方法，同时将每序列缓存内存减少至原来的1/10。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法采用固定的每步直接注意力评分与确定性 top-K 选择，导致无法恢复被错误淘汰的细微但重要的令牌，尤其在长上下文和代理型大模型工作负载中表现不佳。

Method: 提出 Nexus Sampling，结合 Nexus scoring（迭代遍历直接注意力以发现桥接令牌）与加权水库采样（基于包含概率而非确定性选择），实现更灵活、可逆的缓存管理。

Result: 在 80% 缓存淘汰率下，Nexus Sampling 在 LongBench 上性能仅比密集注意力低 1%，并在检索密集型任务中显著优于 top-K 基线；同时每序列缓存内存降低达 10 倍。

Conclusion: Nexus Sampling 在不依赖训练的情况下，通过动态、概率性的缓存淘汰机制，显著提升了长上下文推理中重要信息的保留能力，是应对高淘汰率场景的有效方案。

Abstract: Long-context and agentic LLM workloads push the KV cache past any fixed memory budget, forcing the inference stack to permanently evict tokens at every step of a continuous-inference stream. Existing methods all share the same template, a per-step direct-attention score followed by deterministic top-$K$ selection, which converts a single below-cutoff step into an irreversible verdict and permanently erases any subtly important token that direct attention cannot single out from noise. To address this challenge, we propose Nexus Sampling, a training-free eviction method that pairs Nexus scoring, an iterative walk over direct attention that surfaces bridge tokens, with weighted reservoir sampling, which retains tokens with inclusion probability in place of deterministic top-$K$. Theoretically, we show that Nexus Sampling dominates deterministic top-$K$ in long-run survival of subtly important tokens. Empirically, at 80% KV cache eviction, Nexus Sampling matches dense attention within 1% on LongBench while outperforming top-$K$ baselines on retrieval-heavy tasks, with up to 10x smaller per-sequence cache memory.

### [212] [Learning to Trigger: Reinforcement Learning at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23993)

TL;DR: 本文将在线阈值调优问题建模为序列决策问题，利用强化学习（RL）代理根据实时数据流调整触发阈值，以在保持背景率稳定的同时最大化信号效率。提出两种改进的组过滤策略优化方法（GFPO-F 和 GFPO-FR），确保训练过程中的背景率可行性。在模拟和真实碰撞数据（CMS Run 283408）上验证，该方法在 $H_T$ 触发器上使符合容忍区间的时长比例提升48%（模拟）和56%（真实），在异常检测触发器上分别提升28%，并带来最高达2%的信号效率增益。这是首次在真实LHC数据上实现基于强化学习的触发控制。

Abstract: High-throughput scientific facilities such as the Large Hadron Collider depend on real-time event filtering (\textit{triggering}) under tight constraints on bandwidth, latency, and storage. In practice, trigger menus are largely static and hand-tuned and can become suboptimal as detector conditions, pileup, and background composition drift over time. We cast online threshold tuning as a sequential decision-making problem: a reinforcement learning agent ingests streaming summaries of recent rates and signal-sensitive features and updates trigger thresholds to maximize signal efficiency while tracking a target background rate within a tolerance band. We adapt Group-Filtered Policy Optimization (GFPO) to streaming control and introduce two variants (GFPO-F, GFPO-FR) that enforce background rate feasibility during training. On a benchmark that emulates realistic collider operation, we study two representative triggers: a total transverse energy ($H_{T}$) trigger sensitive to pileup variation, and an anomaly-detection (AD) trigger based on reconstruction loss for rare or non-standard signatures. On Monte Carlo streams, our agent increases the fraction of in-tolerance time intervals by 48\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD), with a cumulative gain of up to 2\% in signal efficiency on those in-tolerance intervals. Transferring from simulation to \emph{real} collision data (CMS Run 283408), the same agent, without fine-tuning, achieves a 56\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD) in-tolerance improvement over baselines, with further signal-efficiency gain on both triggers. To our knowledge, this is the \emph{first} demonstration of RL-based trigger control on real Large Hadron Collider collision data. Code is available at https://github.com/Zixind/GFPO\_LHC.

The uniform distribution has emerged as a strong policy regularization target for this purpose, but it regularizes equally toward all actions regardless of their viability. We introduce EMAgnet, which instead regularizes toward an exponential moving average (EMA) of the last-iterate policy's parameters, providing an adaptive regularization target that evolves with the agent's improving strategy. ### [214] [Cyclic Denoising Reveals Ultrastable Memories in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24000)
*Rishabh Sharma,Stefano Martiniani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出循环去噪（cyclic denoising）作为一种针对图像扩散模型的提取攻击方法，通过在可控噪声幅度下反复进行正向和反向扩散，揭示标准采样难以触及的模型学习分布区域。该方法受无序固体中随机组织的启发，驱动样本趋向具有广泛稳定性的吸引子，其中最深的吸引子表现出超稳定性，即使经历几乎完全破坏仍能恢复，并持续数千次噪声-去噪循环。这些吸引子大多对应于训练数据中的记忆图像，如商业照片、品牌水印和网络爬取痕迹。该攻击仅需采样级别控制，无需梯度、权重检查、提示词、描述或训练数据先验知识，且为全无条件协议，与依赖大规模生成和后处理过滤的生成-筛选攻击不同。在Stable Diffusion v1.4和像素空间DDPM中均验证了该现象，显示跨潜在空间与像素空间的一致性。在不同噪声幅度下观察到类似屈服的相变：低噪声循环产生平凡吸收固定点或极限环，而高噪声引发重组、盆地跳跃及在结构化记忆吸引子盆地中的长期滞留。还发现层级部分吸收、提示稳定盆地以及跨初始条件的吸引子集合普遍性。结果表明，循环去噪既是生成景观的物理启发式探测工具，也是记忆审计的实际手段，对隐私、版权合规和模型指纹识别具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像扩散模型可能隐含记忆训练数据中的敏感内容（如品牌水印、网页爬取内容），但缺乏有效手段探测其记忆行为。传统生成-筛选攻击依赖大量提示生成与后处理过滤，效率低且需外部信息。因此需要一种无需提示、不依赖梯度或权重访问、可直接暴露模型内部记忆结构的新方法。

Method: 提出循环去噪（cyclic denoising）：在可控噪声水平下重复执行前向扩散（加噪）与反向扩散（去噪）过程，通过动态演化探索生成模型的潜在能量景观。利用采样器级别的控制，不使用梯度、不访问模型权重、不依赖提示或标签，实现全无条件运行。通过观察样本在多次迭代后的收敛状态，识别出稳定吸引子，进而判断是否对应于训练数据中的记忆内容。

Result: 在Stable Diffusion v1.4和像素空间DDPM上均成功检测到多个超稳定吸引子，其形态与训练集中真实图像高度一致，包括商业图片、品牌水印和网络爬取痕迹。随着噪声幅度增加，系统出现类似材料屈服的相变行为：低噪声下趋于平凡固定点，高噪声下进入复杂结构吸引子盆地，表现出盆地跳跃和长时滞留。此外，观察到层级部分吸收、提示增强的稳定盆地，以及吸引子集对初始条件的普遍性。该方法在多种架构与空间中具有一致有效性。

Conclusion: 循环去噪是一种高效、通用且无需先验知识的提取攻击方法，能够有效揭示扩散模型中的记忆内容。它不仅为理解生成模型的内在动力学提供物理类比视角，更具备实际应用价值，可用于隐私泄露检测、版权合规审查和模型指纹识别，推动生成模型的安全与责任发展。

Abstract: We introduce cyclic denoising -- repeated forward and reverse diffusion at controlled noise amplitudes -- as an extraction attack for image diffusion models. Inspired by random organization in disordered solids, cyclic denoising exposes regions of the learned distribution that are largely inaccessible to standard sampling. The dynamics drive samples toward attractors with a broad stability spectrum. The deepest attractors are ultrastable: they regenerate after near-total corruption and persist through thousands of noising-denoising cycles. Many of these attractors correspond to memorized training images, including stock photographs, brand watermarks, and web-crawl artifacts. The attack requires only sampler-level control, with no gradients, weight inspection, prompts, captions, or prior knowledge of the training data. Unlike generate-and-filter attacks, which rely on large-scale prompted generation and post-hoc similarity or membership-inference filtering, our main protocol is fully unconditioned. We demonstrate the phenomenon in Stable Diffusion v1.4 and in a pixel-space DDPM, showing consistent behavior across latent- and pixel-space diffusion models. Across noise amplitudes, we observe a yielding-like transition: low-amplitude cycling produces trivial absorbing fixed points or limit cycles, while larger amplitudes induce rearrangements, basin hopping, and long-lived trapping in structured memorized attractor basins. We also observe hierarchical partial absorption, prompt-stabilized basins, and cross-initial-condition universality of the recovered attractor set. Our results therefore show that cyclic denoising is both a physics-inspired probe of generative landscapes and a practical tool for memorization auditing, with implications for privacy, copyright compliance, and model fingerprinting.

</details>


### [215] [Fast and Slow Variational Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24007)
*Subarnaduti Paul,Yohan Jung,Mohammad Emtiyaz Khan,Siddharth Swaroop,Thomas Möllenhoff,Martin Mundt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种名为CoVON的新优化器，通过在IVON基础上引入过去后验作为先验，实现快速与慢速适应的平衡，有效缓解持续学习中的知识漂移问题，在多个任务中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化器缺乏内在的持续适应机制，难以在保持稳定性的同时实现足够的可塑性，因此需要一种能模拟生物神经机制的优化策略。

Method: 基于VCL框架，利用历史后验合并为慢适应先验，并结合IVON优化器实现快权重更新，形成新型优化器CoVON。

Result: CoVON在领域增量学习、持续预训练和大语言模型微调任务中均表现出色，优于现有VCL优化器及权重正则化策略。

Conclusion: CoVON通过融合慢适应与快适应机制，显著提升了深度网络在持续学习场景下的性能，具有良好的实用性和扩展性。

Abstract: Continual learning remains a major challenge for modern deep networks, partly because commonly used optimizers lack inherent mechanisms for continual adaptation. One such natural mechanism is fast and slow adaptation to balance stability and plasticity. This mechanism has deep roots in neuroscience and biology, but there is no consensus on how to best incorporate it in commonly used optimizers. Here, we show that this can be easily done via the VCL framework, where past posteriors are used as priors in the future. Our key idea is to incorporate slow adaptation via merging of past posteriors to slow down the drift in the knowledge as learning progresses. The merged posterior is then used as the prior in the VCL update to implement the fast-weight updates. These steps can be seamlessly implemented in the IVON optimizer, whose form and costs are nearly identical to that of Adam. We call this new optimizer the Continual IVON (CoVON) optimizer and show that it not only consistently improves over existing VCL optimizers, but also performs better than other weight-regularization strategies across domain-incremental learning, continual pre-training, and fine-tuning of large language models.

### [216] [You Don't Need to Run Every Eval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24020)
*Yuchen Zeng,Dimitris Papailiopoulos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现，84个前沿模型在133个基准测试上的评分矩阵具有近似秩-2特性，即模型在所有基准上的表现主要由两个核心因素决定。基于此，作者提出BenchPress方法，通过logit空间的秩-2矩阵补全技术，以平均4.6分误差恢复缺失评分，并引入置信度层判断预测可靠性。研究进一步发现，仅需5个基准（如GPQA-D、HLE等）即可在3.93分误差内重建模型整体评分卡；更节省预算的5个基准组合也能实现4.55分内的高精度预测。相关数据、代码和交互工具均已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型模型评估依赖大量基准测试，但重复评估成本高且冗余。本文旨在探究是否可减少评估数量，通过发现评分模式的低秩结构来高效推断模型性能。

Method: 构建包含2,604个评分单元（填充率23.3%）的公开评分矩阵，利用矩阵分解技术验证其秩-2特性；设计BenchPress方法进行logit空间的秩-2矩阵补全，并引入置信度机制；通过交叉验证筛选出能代表整体性能的关键基准集。

Result: BenchPress可将缺失评分预测误差控制在4.6分以内；5个关键基准可实现3.93分内的整体性能重建；更经济的5个基准组合亦能达到4.55分误差水平。

Conclusion: 模型在多个基准上的表现存在高度共性，仅需少量代表性评测即可准确推断其综合性能。该发现为高效模型评估提供了新范式，显著降低评估成本并提升效率。

Abstract: A modern model release reports scores on 40+ benchmarks and the same evaluations were run many more times before it: to track training progress, compare design choices, and select the checkpoint for the release. But do we need to run every eval? We compile a public score matrix of 84 frontier models on 133 benchmarks (2,604 cells, 23.3% filled) and find it is approximately rank-2: a model's scores across all 133 benchmarks are largely determined by just two numbers. We confirm this in two ways: scores hidden from the matrix are best recovered using two factors, and two factors already explain over 90% of the variation among models on the benchmarks they share. Building on this, we design BenchPress: a logit-space rank-2 matrix completion method that recovers held-out scores to within 4.6 points, and a confidence layer that says when each prediction can be trusted. Using BenchPress, we find a subset of five benchmarks {GPQA-D, HLE, Codeforces, MMLU-Pro, ARC-AGI-1} that can recover the rest of a model's public scorecard to within 3.93 points. For a tighter inference budget, a cheaper set {GPQA-D, MMLU-Pro, Aider Polyglot, MATH-500, AIME 2026} can predict a model's evals to within 4.55. We release the score matrix, the BenchPress code, and an interactive tool that predicts any model's score on any benchmark.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前条件生成中，分类器自由引导（CFG）虽能提升条件一致性，但过强引导会降低生成多样性与分布覆盖范围。现有方法缺乏对引导调度在逆向轨迹中的动态控制机制，且引导诱导的分布并非简单的固定时间倾斜分布，因此需要一种新的理论框架来优化引导策略。

Method: 提出一个信息论框架，利用干净终点作为参考，通过轨迹级公式从样本和得分评估中估计目标函数，从而优化引导调度，实现对条件一致性与分布覆盖度的精细控制。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于信息论的CFG调度优化框架有效缓解了条件生成中的一致性-覆盖度权衡问题，为可控生成提供了更灵活、自适应的引导策略。

Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved strong performance in image, text-to-image, and video generation, where conditional generation is often controlled by classifier-free guidance (CFG). CFG improves condition consistency by increasing a guidance weight, but stronger guidance typically reduces diversity and distributional coverage. It remains unclear how this consistency-coverage trade-off should be controlled across the reverse trajectory, since the distribution induced by CFG is not simply the fixed-time tilted distribution given by the guided score field. To address this issue, we propose an information-theoretic framework for CFG schedule optimization. Our approach uses a clean endpoint reference to specify the desired consistency-coverage trade-off, while optimizing the actual distribution induced by the guided sampler toward this reference. We derive trajectory-level formulas to estimate the objective from samples and score evaluations, avoiding explicit density estimation. On ImageNet-512 with EDM-XXL and COCO with SD-XL, the learned schedules achieve competitive or improved trade-offs over constant guidance and allocate guidance selectively across noise levels.

### [218] [RoPE-Aware Bit Allocation for KV-Cache Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24033)
*Fengfeng Liang,Yuechen Zhang,Jiaya Jia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Block-GTQ，一种基于TurboQuant-MSE的RoPE感知型关键缓存量化比特分配方法。针对传统方法将键视为扁平向量的问题，利用RoPE中频率块的能量特性，为不同块动态分配比特，提升注意力日志的保真度。在多个模型和任务上，相比均匀量化，显著降低MAE（32-80%），大幅提高长上下文推理、检索与理解性能，并实现高压缩比与高效推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低比特键缓存量化方法将每个键视为扁平向量，忽略了RoPE编码下键对注意力日志的贡献具有位置依赖性且由二维频率块组成的特点。高能量频率块对量化误差更敏感，应分配更多比特，因此需要一种能感知RoPE结构的分块比特分配策略。

Method: Block-GTQ基于TQ-MSE，为每层每头的每个RoPE频率块计算无标签能量评分，通过贪婪边际增益算法进行整数比特宽度分配，实现块级自适应比特分配。同时支持压缩缓存服务路径，优化实际部署效率。

Result: 在10个模型的诊断测试中，相较于均匀TQ-MSE，在相同比特预算下，Block-GTQ将每层平均绝对误差（MAE）降低32%-80%；在2和3 b/dim K-only量化下，所有367个层均表现更优。下游任务如NIAH和LongBench-EN得分显著提升，且在无fp16近期键缓冲时仍保持良好性能。在单张H800 GPU上，使用打包缓存的K3V3配置实现3.24倍压缩，速度达fp16 FlashAttention2的1.34倍，峰值内存从56.31GB降至19.85GB，支持至512K上下文。

Conclusion: Block-GTQ通过引入RoPE感知的分块比特分配机制，显著提升了低比特键缓存量化在长上下文场景下的精度与效率，是实现高性能、高压缩比大模型推理的关键技术。代码已开源。

Abstract: Existing low-bit KV-cache quantizers often treat each cached key as a flat vector. Under RoPE, however, a key's contribution to a future attention logit decomposes into a position-dependent sum over two-dimensional frequency blocks. This makes key-cache quantization a block-wise bit-allocation problem: high-energy RoPE blocks are more sensitive to quantization error and should receive more bits. We introduce Block-GTQ, a RoPE-aware bit allocator for key-cache quantization built on TurboQuant-MSE(TQ-MSE). For each layer and KV head, Block-GTQ computes a label-free energy score for each RoPE block and greedily allocates integer bit widths by marginal gain. Under matched K/V bit budgets, Block-GTQ better preserves RoPE query-key logits on a ten-model diagnostic panel, cutting per-layer MAE by 32-80% at 2 and 3 b/dim K-only quantization and winning all 367/367 layer comparisons against uniform TQ-MSE. These fidelity gains translate to stronger downstream long-context retrieval, understanding, and reasoning. At K2V2 on Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, Block-GTQ raises the six-task NIAH average from 70.6 to 97.4, and the LongBench-EN average from 36.87 to 53.31. On AIME 2024/2025 with DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B, without an fp16 recent-key buffer, Block-GTQ at K3V2 scores 51.7/37.5, close to fp16's 54.2/37.9, whereas uniform TQ-MSE collapses to 0.0/0.0. We further implement a packed-cache serving path. On a single H800 GPU with Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct, packed K3V3 achieves 3.24x KV-cache compression with fp16-comparable quality, runs 1.34x faster than fp16 FlashAttention2 at 128K context, reduces peak memory from 56.31 GB to 19.85 GB, and remains feasible at 256K and 512K where fp16 OOMs. Code is available at https://github.com/JIA-Lab-research/blockgtq.

### [220] [RAVEN: A Regime-Aware Variable-context Expert Network for Financial Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24062)
*Cheng He,Zhenyu Guan,Xijie Liang,Defu Lian,Jiajia Li,Enhong Chen,Patrick P. C. Lee,Geng Hu,Zehao Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RAVEN提出一种自适应时间上下文的混合专家框架，通过动态确定非平稳价格过程的最佳回溯窗口，解决金融时间序列预测中固定上下文窗口不匹配的问题。其核心机制包括基于逆时序重要性评分的累积重要性阈值（CIT）生成嵌套前缀窗口，分层路由至专用专家，并结合全局压缩表示（GCR）保持全局时序一致性。引入相关性感知加权（CAW）对不同长度专家输出进行校准，提升聚合效果。在沪深300、标普500指数收益预测及基金销售预测任务中显著优于现有方法，相关性提升最高达20.2%，均方误差降低18.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融时间序列具有非平稳性、极低信噪比和依赖状态的时序依赖特征，现有SOTA模型采用固定上下文窗口无法适配时变最优回溯周期，导致建模偏差。

Method: 提出RAVEN框架，利用累积重要性阈值（CIT）从逆时序数据中自动识别关键时间片段，构建嵌套的连续窗口；每个窗口被路由至对应尺度的专家网络；并行运行全局压缩表示（GCR）以保留长期依赖关系；通过相关性感知加权（CAW）对专家输出进行加权融合，减少冗余与冲突。

Result: 在累计对数收益预测（HS300、S&P500）和基金销售预测任务中，RAVEN达到SOTA性能，相比基线提升Pearson相关系数9.2%（HS300）和20.2%（S&P500），MSE降低18.2%（基金销售）；在四个PEMS交通基准上16项指标中有14项最优。

Conclusion: RAVEN通过动态自适应上下文选择与结构化专家协作机制，有效应对金融时间序列中的非平稳性和复杂依赖结构，在多个真实场景下展现出卓越的预测能力与泛化性能。

Abstract: Financial time series forecasting presents structural challenges absent from standard benchmarks. Log-returns are non-stationary, exhibit exceptionally low signal-to-noise (SNR) ratios, and are governed by regime-dependent temporal dependencies. We identify a key limitation of state-of-the-art (SOTA) time series models in financial settings. A fixed context window is mismatched to the time-varying optimal look-back of non-stationary price processes. We propose the Regime-Aware Variable-context Expert Network (RAVEN), a Mixture-of-Experts framework designed to adaptively determine the temporal context for each input sample. Instead of relying on a fixed look-back horizon, RAVEN constructs a hierarchy of nested contiguous windows whose lengths are determined by the data itself. Specifically, RAVEN scores patches by learned importance in reverse chronological order and applies the Cumulative Importance Thresholding (CIT) mechanism to derive nested prefix windows, each routed to a scale-specialized expert. A Global Compressed Representation (GCR) branch runs in parallel over the full context, preserving global temporal coherence that local experts cannot guarantee. Because the nested routing induces structured overlap among expert inputs, we introduce a Correlation-Aware Weighting (CAW) to align variable-length expert outputs and penalize pairwise cosine similarity prior to aggregation. Experiments on cumulative log-return prediction (HS300, S&P500) and fund sales forecasting demonstrate that RAVEN achieves SOTA performances, improves Pearson correlation by 9.2% on HS300 and 20.2% on S&P500, and reduces MSE by 18.2% on fund sales forecasting, while achieving the best results in 14 of 16 metrics on four PEMS traffic benchmarks.

### [221] [Blockwise Policy-Drift Gating for On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24084)
*Liwen Zheng,Haiyun Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轻量级的学生端旧-当前策略漂移控制器（blockwise policy-drift gating），用于改进基于回放的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）。该方法通过计算行为学生与当前学生在采样路径上的对数概率差异，并在固定块内聚合这些差异，生成去关联的、均值归一化的门控信号来重加权OPD的位置损失，不改变教师目标、教师top-K支持或回放策略。在六个变体的Qwen3数学推理基准测试中，64令牌块门控将采样令牌OPD的平均通过率（pass@8）从0.4978提升至0.5160，且在Teacher-TopK/LSM设置下表现最佳，验证了局部旧-当前策略漂移作为实用控制信号的有效性，建议将其作为提升求解率鲁棒性的默认策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有采样令牌的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）在长时序推理任务中表现脆弱，而局部教师支持匹配虽有效但存在局限。本文旨在解决因策略漂移导致的训练不稳定问题，尤其是在回放轨迹重复使用场景下。

Method: 提出块级策略漂移门控机制：计算行为学生与当前学生在采样路径上的对数概率差，按固定块（如64令牌）聚合，生成去关联的均值归一化门控信号，用于重加权OPD损失，保持教师信号和回放策略不变。

Result: 在六项数学推理任务上，64令牌块门控使采样令牌OPD的平均pass@8从0.4978提升至0.5160；在Teacher-TopK/LSM设置下，块64方案在四项基准测试中取得最高平均通过率，显著提升了求解率的稳定性和性能。

Conclusion: 局部旧-当前策略漂移可作为回放式OPD中的有效控制信号，块级门控是一种简单且高效的默认策略，能显著提升长时序推理任务中策略蒸馏的鲁棒性与性能。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student policy using teacher signals computed on trajectories sampled by the student itself. Recent work shows that sampled-token OPD can be fragile on long-horizon reasoning tasks and that local teacher-support matching is a simple and effective repair. This paper introduces blockwise policy-drift gating, a lightweight student-only old-current drift controller for OPD under rollout reuse. The method computes log-probability shifts between the behavior student and the current student on the sampled token path, aggregates these shifts over fixed blocks or spans, and uses the resulting detached, mean-normalized gates to reweight OPD position losses. It does not change teacher targets, teacher top-K supports, or the rollout policy. In a six-variant Qwen3 math reasoning benchmark with a uniform 200-step training budget for all trained variants, we use pass@8 as the primary problem-level solve-rate metric. Fixed 64-token block gating improves sampled-token OPD mean pass@8 from 0.4978 to 0.5160 across AIME24, AIME25, MATH500, and AMC23. On Teacher-TopK/LSM, Block64 gives the best four-benchmark mean pass@8 among trained students. The results identify local old-current policy drift as a practical control signal for reused OPD rollouts and motivate block-level gating as a simple default for improving solve-rate robustness.

</details>


### [222] [NeuroSonic: Conditional Flow Matching for EEG-to-Speech Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24087)
*Wenhao Gao,Yifan Wang,Yijia Ma,Carl Yang,Wen Li,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NeuroSonic提出了一种基于条件流匹配的框架，用于从头皮脑电图（EEG）重建连续语音。该方法通过学习一个确定性的概率流速度场，将噪声污染的音频状态在EEG条件引导下传输至清晰语音，避免了迭代随机采样，提升了重建稳定性与质量。在CineBrain和EAV数据集上的跨被试评估表明，该方法在分布真实性、频谱保真度和感知质量方面显著优于主流的GAN、扩散模型和均值流基线，尤其在含伪影段落中优势明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG信号具有空间弥散、弱且高度可变的特点，而语音具有强谐波与时间结构，两者之间的不匹配导致传统波形回归不稳定，且随机多步生成对伪影依赖性和个体差异敏感。因此需要一种更稳定、高效的方法来实现高质量的EEG-to-speech重建。

Method: NeuroSonic采用条件流匹配框架，将EEG与音频映射到共享标记空间，使用时序条件门控Transformer参数化传输常微分方程，学习一个确定性的概率流速度场，实现从噪声音频状态到干净语音的直接、非迭代变换。

Result: 在CineBrain和EAV数据集上，神经声学模型在分布真实性、频谱保真度和感知质量方面均优于现有基线方法，特别是在伪影严重的片段中表现突出，整体感知质量提升最高达26.3%。

Conclusion: 确定性条件传输提供了一种稳定有效的EEG驱动语音重建范式，能够有效应对信号变异性和伪影干扰，显著提升重建性能。

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous speech from scalp electroencephalography (EEG) remains fundamentally challenging. EEG provides a weak, spatially diffuse, and highly variable measurement of distributed cortical activity, whereas speech is organized as a coherent acoustic trajectory with strong harmonic and temporal structure. The resulting mismatch makes waveform regression unstable and causes stochastic multi-step generation to be sensitive to artifact-dependent conditioning and subject variability. We introduce NeuroSonic, a conditional flow-matching framework for EEG-to-speech reconstruction. Instead of predicting waveforms directly or refining them through stochastic denoising, NeuroSonic learns a deterministic probability-flow velocity field that transports a noise-corrupted acoustic state toward clean speech under EEG conditioning. EEG and audio are embedded into a shared token space and processed by a time-conditioned gated Transformer that parameterizes the transport ordinary differential equation. This formulation models trajectory evolution explicitly while avoiding iterative stochastic sampling. We evaluate NeuroSonic on the CineBrain and EAV benchmarks under cross-subject evaluation. Across both datasets, the proposed method improves distributional realism, spectral fidelity, and perceptual quality over representative GAN-, diffusion-, and mean-flow baselines, with up to a 26.3\% gain in overall perceptual quality. The performance gap is most evident in artifact-heavy segments, where conditioning variability is strongest. These findings indicate that deterministic conditional transport provides a stable and effective formulation for EEG-driven speech reconstruction. Code is available at https://github.com/Y-Research-SBU/NeuroSonic/ .

### [223] [FedUP: One-Shot Federated Unlearning via Centroid-Guided Plug-in Filters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24113)

Abstract: Federated unlearning (FU) is critical for complying with legal mandates like the right to be forgotten in decentralized systems, yet current methods face a persistent dilemma between non-target knowledge loss and high request latency. To resolve these issues, we propose FedUP, a one-shot federated unlearning framework utilizing lightweight pluggable filters that act as a "knowledge funnel" to screen out target data while preserving original model performance. By freezing original model parameters and training filters at the server side using differentially private (DP)-protected class centroid samples, FedUP bypasses the need for multi-round client-server communication and complex retraining, reducing unlearning latency from minutes to mere seconds. Additionally, the framework's pluggable architecture ensures inherent reversibility, enabling the seamless restoration of forgotten knowledge by simply removing the filters. ### [224] [When Top-1 Fails: Calibrating LoRA Monitors for Masked Diffusion LMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24119)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在三个DLM家族共816个LoRA/PEFT配置上测试顶1集中度与最大LoRA梯度范数的表现，通过对比实际崩溃情况与预警信号响应，分析其可靠性，并在独立数据集上优化阈值以评估性能。

Result: 顶1集中度在无任何真实崩溃的情况下持续触发警报，精确率为0；而最大梯度范数在特定数据集上表现出良好性能（精确率0.68，F1=0.79），但结果受限于短时程和特定模型族。

Conclusion: 顶1概率集中度不适合作为PEFT训练崩溃的预警信号，应弃用；建议采用早期记录的最大梯度范数，并针对不同DLM家族校准阈值，用于短时程训练过程监控。

We test top-1 argmax concentration as a collapse warning. Across 816 LoRA/PEFT configurations from three DLM families, the warning fires for every configuration while logs record 0/816 actual collapses at the 200 step horizon, giving zero precision. The cause is pre-equilibrium saturation: top-1 concentration is already high before optimization and quickly becomes insensitive to final training stability. We then evaluate max LoRA gradient norm, a parameter-side signal that samples gradient routing rather than token concentration. On a pooled held-out LLaDA-family split, a train-optimized threshold identifies top-decile final-loss configurations with precision 0.68 and F1=0.79, above the all-positive top-1 baseline even at the lower split-bootstrap confidence bound. Autoregressive controls and cross-family threshold failures bound the result to short-horizon DLM-LoRA inspection rather than a universal collapse detector. Workflow: drop top-1 as a PEFT alarm, log max-gradient early in training, and calibrate thresholds per DLM family before routing runs for inspection.
